infoBubble[e.a.toUpperCase()]=='undefined'){lat_a=e.label[1].lat;lng_a=e.label[1].lng;color=(e.a_minoan)?'#e03a3e':'#003a70';infoBubble[e.a.toUpperCase()]=new InfoBubble({map:map,content:'<span  class=\"bb_content\" style=\" background: '+color+';color: #fff;padding: 5px;border-radius: 5px;line-height: 14px;display: block;overflow: hidden;text-align: center;\">'+e.a+'</span>',position:new google.maps.LatLng({lat:lat_a,lng:lng_a}),shadowStyle:0,padding:0,height:25,backgroundColor:'transparent',borderRadius:5,arrowSize:10,borderWidth:0,borderColor:'transparent',disableAutoPan:true,hideCloseButton:true,arrowPosition:30,backgroundClassName:'transparent',arrowStyle:2});infoBubble[e.a.toUpperCase()].open();}if(typeof infoBubble[e.da.toUpperCase()]=='undefined'){lat_da=e.label[0].lat;lng_da=e.label[0].lng;color=(e.da_minoan)?'#e03a3e':'#003a70';infoBubble[e.da.toUpperCase()]=new InfoBubble({map:map,content:'<span class=\"bb_content\" style=\" background: '+color+';color: #fff;padding: 5px;border-radius: 5px;line-height: 14px;display: block;overflow: hidden;text-align: center;\">'+e.da+'</span>',position:new google.maps.LatLng({lat:lat_da,lng:lng_da}),shadowStyle:0,padding:0,height:25,backgroundColor:'transparent',borderRadius:5,arrowSize:10,borderWidth:0,borderColor:'transparent',disableAutoPan:true,hideCloseButton:true,arrowPosition:30,backgroundClassName:'transparent',arrowStyle:2});infoBubble[e.da.toUpperCase()].open();}});var marker;window.port_line=per_port;$.each(porti,function(i,p){marker=new google.maps.Marker({position:new google.maps.LatLng(p['lat'],p['lon']),map:map,icon:'https://www.grimaldi-lines.com/assets/frontend/theme/images/marker.gif'});google.maps.event.addListener(marker,'mouseover',(function(marker,i){return function(){clearMap();$.each(window.port_line[p['title'].toUpperCase()],function(a,b){b.setMap(map);});dest=destinazioni[parseInt(p['destinazione'])];var html='';$.each(tratte_per_porto[p['entity_id']],function(i,e){var pp=e.porto_partenza;var pa=e.porto_arrivo;if(pa.title.toUpperCase()==p['title'].toUpperCase()){var appoggio=pp;pp=pa;pa=appoggio;}var name_partenza=pp.title;var name_arrivo=pa.title;if(e.servita=='48'){link='http://www.minoan.gr/it';}else{link='https://booking.grimaldi-lines.com/?c=GRI&l=it&l1='+pp.code+'-'+pa.code+'&d1=&l2=&d2=';}html+='<li><a href=\"'+link+'\" target=\"_blank\">'+name_partenza+' / '+name_arrivo+'</a></li>';infoBubble[name_partenza.toUpperCase()].open();infoBubble[name_arrivo.toUpperCase()].open();});$('#info .content .panel-heading h5').html(p['title']);$('#info .content .panel-heading a').attr('href',p['link']);$('#info .content .panel-body ul').html(html);$('#info .content .panel-body .dest').hide();if(typeof dest!='undefined'){}$('#info').css('left',0);}})(marker,i));});}function clearMap(){for(var item in window.port_line){for(var e in window.port_line[item]){window.port_line[item.toUpperCase()][e].setMap(null);}}for(var name in infoBubble){$('.bb_content').css('background','#f1f1f1').css('color','#003a70');}}$(document).delegate('#info .chiudi','click',function(){for(var item in window.port_line){for(var e in window.port_line[item]){if(window.port_line[item][e].visualizza)window.port_line[item][e].setMap(map);}}for(var name in infoBubble){infoBubble[name].open();}$('#info').css('left','-300px');});</script>  <div id=\"mm-blocker\" class=\"mm-slideout\"></div></body>"}
